			<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 9pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: center; margin: 0pt 0pt 2pt; text-indent: 0pt;">The <ix:nonNumeric contextRef="d20248K_StatementClassOfStockAxis_WarrantsToAcquireOnehalfOfOneShareOfCommonStockFor1150PerShare" format="ixt-sec:exchnameen" name="dei:SecurityExchangeName" id="ixv-301">Nasdaq</ix:nonNumeric>&#160;Capital Market</div>

</tbody></table>

			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><i>Cash and cash equivalents of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="1x1" data-tblname="394188" data-tblv="20" id="led394188F2024471715104029096" originalfact="$ 21,682,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$21.7 million</a> as of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="20" id="led391585F2023771691438175058">June 30, 2024</a></i></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><b>SALT LAKE CITY, August 7,&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="391587" data-tblv="20" id="led391587F20241261708978150778">2024</a></b> -- Clene Inc. (Nasdaq: CLNN) (along with its subsidiaries, &#8220;Clene&#8221;) and its wholly owned subsidiary Clene Nanomedicine Inc., a late clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on revolutionizing the treatment of neurodegenerative diseases, including amyotrophic lateral sclerosis (ALS) and multiple sclerosis (MS), today announced its second quarter 2024 financial results and provided recent updates on its CNM-Au8<sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">&#174;</sup> programs.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&#8220;We are approaching our next FDA interaction focused on the regulatory path forward to potentially bring CNM-Au8 to people living with ALS,&#8221; said Rob Etherington, President and CEO of Clene. &#8220;With this imminent timing, we are optimistic about the possibility of submitting a new drug application later this year. Our utmost priority is to help patients and their families for whom time is critical.&#8221;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><b><a data-tblloc="44x1" data-tblname="391587" data-tblv="20" id="led391587F20241261708978169854">Second</a> Quarter <a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="391587" data-tblv="20" id="led391587F20241261708978158894">2024</a> and Recent Operating Highlights</b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><i><b>CNM-Au8 for the treatment of ALS</b></i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">In June, the Company presented new long-term CNM-Au8 treatment results for survival and neurofilament light (NfL) levels from the HEALEY ALS Platform Trial open label extension (OLE) at the European Network for the Cure of ALS (ENCALS) meeting in Stockholm, Sweden. The data highlights up to 42 months of survival follow-up and 76 weeks of long-term NfL biomarker results, including a NfL responder subset (CNM-Au8 NfL Responders) from the HEALEY ALS Platform Trial who had consistent and sustained NfL reductions, comprising nearly half of all CNM-Au8 patients.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">The data demonstrated improved survival compared to matched PRO-ACT controls as well as continued significant decline in plasma NfL levels in CNM-Au8 treated patients.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><b>Improved Survival Compared to Matched PRO-ACT Controls:</b> Survival analyses of participants originally randomized to CNM-Au8 30 mg treatment (n=59) and ex-placebo to CNM-Au8 (n=11) compared to matched PRO-ACT controls up to 3.5 years post-baseline.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 6pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt; vertical-align: top;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 27pt; vertical-align: top;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">Approximately 60% decreased risk of death in CNM-Au8 30 mg treated patients compared to matched PRO-ACT controls up to 3.5 years of follow-up; covariate-adjusted hazard ratio (HR): 0.431 (95% CI: 0.276-0.672), p-value = 0.0002.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;"><b>Reduced NfL Biomarker Levels in CNM-Au8 NfL Responders:</b> CNM-Au8 NfL Responder Subset: The CNM-Au8 NfL Responder analysis was completed to identify NfL decreases in participants who showed consistent NfL declines (n=55). CNM-Au8 NfL Responders were defined as participants who had all post-baseline measures with an NfL decrease or repeated declines of at least 10 pg/mL following the start of CNM-Au8 treatment.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 6pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 27pt;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">CNM-Au8 NfL Responders demonstrated an average NfL reduction of 28%, which is suggestive of decreased axonal loss on an ongoing basis; geometric mean ratio (GMR) at week 76 change vs. baseline: 0.72, (95% CI: 0.67 &#8211; 0.79), p &lt; 0.0001.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 6pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 27pt;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">The NfL results are based on earlier announced analyses of plasma NfL collected from participants (n=99) in the OLE who were treated with CNM-Au8 30 mg through week 76 compared to participants treated with placebo for 24 weeks prior to crossing over to active treatment for up to 52 weeks. Long-term treatment with CNM-Au8 30 mg resulted in continued significant decline of plasma NfL levels. The GMR vs. placebo at week 76 was 0.841, 95% CI: 0.73 &#8211; 0.98, p = 0.023.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<div class="PGBK" style="width: 100%; margin-left: 0pt; margin-right: 0pt">
<div class="PGFTR" style="text-align: center; width: 100%">
<div class="hf-row">
<div class="hf-cell PGNUM">&nbsp;</div>
</div>

<hr style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; border: none; width: 100%; height: 2px; color: #000000; background-color: #000000">
<div class="PGHDR" style="text-align: left; width: 100%">
<div class="hf-row">
<div class="hf-cell TOCLink">&nbsp;</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">On July 13, 2024, the Company submitted a briefing book to FDA in advance of a granted Type C interaction expected to occur in the third quarter of 2024. The briefing book contains new post-hoc analyses from two independently conducted Phase 2 clinical trials of CNM-Au8 for the treatment for ALS. This new information supplements the original data previously discussed with the FDA in late 2023 and is intended to guide the planned FDA Type C interaction to discuss an accelerated approval regulatory pathway. The Company plans to publicly announce the topline FDA feedback following the conclusion of the Type C interaction. CNM-Au8 NfL Responders demonstrated a 28% mean reduction in NfL levels compared to baseline, while NfL levels continued to increase in CNM-Au8 NfL non-responders (all doses; GMR difference at week 76 post-baseline: 0.57, 95% CI: 0.50 &#8211; 0.64, p &lt; 0.00001). The analyses of the CNM-Au8 NfL Responders demonstrated efficacy in all-cause mortality, function, and combined assessment of function and survival (CAFS).</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">Late last year, Clene, in collaboration with Columbia University and Synapticure, announced the award of a four-year grant from the National Institute of Neurological Disorders and Stroke (NINDS), part of the National Institutes of Health (NIH), to support an EAP for the Company&#8217;s investigational drug, CNM-Au8 in ALS. The Company enrolled its first EAP patient in June.</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;"><i><b>CNM-Au8 for the treatment of Rett Syndrome</b></i></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">In June, Clene presented new, preliminary data demonstrating the potential of CNM-Au8 as a treatment for Rett Syndrome. at the International Rett Syndrome Foundation 2024 Annual Meeting. The presentation was titled, &#8220;CNM-Au8, a Candidate First-in-Class Nanotherapeutic for Treatment of Rett Syndrome.&#8221; Key findings included:</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 6pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt; vertical-align: top;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 27pt; vertical-align: top;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">Statistically significant improvement in neuronal health (p&lt;0.01), neuron survival (p&lt;0.0001), and neurite lengths (p&lt;0.05) in an in vitro model of Rett Syndrome, and;</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-size: 6pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><i><b>Corporate Update</b></i></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">In July, Clene completed a 1-for-20 reverse stock split. Clene&#8217;s common stock now trades on the Nasdaq Capital Market on a split-adjusted basis under a new CUSIP number 185634201 and the Company&#8217;s existing trading symbol &#8220;CLNN.&#8221; The reverse stock split enabled Clene to regain compliance with the $1.00 minimum closing bid price required for continued listing on the Nasdaq Capital Market. The number of shares of common stock issued and outstanding has been reduced from approximately 128.7 million shares to approximately 6.4 million shares. All outstanding stock options, warrants, rights to restricted stock awards, convertible debt, and contingent earn-out shares entitling their holders to purchase or receive shares of Common Stock were adjusted as a result of the reverse stock split as required by the terms of each security. In addition, the number of shares reserved for issuance pursuant to the Company&#8217;s Amended 2020 Stock Plan were also adjusted.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><b><a data-tblloc="44x1" data-tblname="391587" data-tblv="20" id="led391587F20241261708978169854">Second</a> Quarter <a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="391587" data-tblv="20" id="led391587F20241261708978158894">2024</a>&nbsp;Financial Results</b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; text-align: justify;">Clene&#8217;s cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities totaled <a data-tblloc="1x1" data-tblname="394188" data-tblv="20" id="led394188F20234101683735191273" originalfact="$ 21,682,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$21.7 million</a>&nbsp;as of <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="20" id="led391585F2023771691438175058">June 30, 2024</a>, compared to <a data-tblloc="1x2" data-tblname="394188" data-tblv="20" id="led394188F20234101683735196750" originalfact="$ 35,000,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$35.0 million</a>&nbsp;as of <a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="20" id="led391585F2023771691438188849">December 31, 2023</a>. Clene expects that its resources as of <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="20" id="led391585F2023771691438201114">June 30, 2024</a>, will be sufficient to fund its operations into the fourth quarter of 2024.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">Research and development expenses were&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x1" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="20" id="led391591F20246301722379052671" originalfact="$4,150,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$4.2 million</a>&nbsp;for the quarter ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="20" id="led391585F2023771691438223925">June 30, 2024</a>, compared to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x2" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="20" id="led391591F20246301722379061684" originalfact="$6,615,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$6.6 million</a>&nbsp;for the same period in <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="20" id="led391585F2023771691438229471">2023</a>.&nbsp;The year-over-year decrease was primarily related to reimbursements for expenses incurred since September 2023 from our ongoing ALS EAP funded by a NIH grant for which reimbursements are recorded as an offset to research and development expense, as well as lower expenses related the HEALEY ALS Platform Trial and the RESCUE-ALS, REPAIR-MS, and VISIONARY-MS clinical trials, partially offset by an increase in expenses related to the two ongoing EAPs and planning activities for the RESTORE-ALS Phase 3 clinical trial.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">General and administrative expenses were&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="20" id="led391591F20246301722379270035" originalfact="$3,314,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$3.3 million</a>&nbsp;for the quarter ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="20" id="led391585F2023771691438223925">June 30, 2024</a>, compared to <a data-tblloc="9x2" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="20" id="led391591F20246301722379278980" originalfact="$3,924,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$3.9 million</a>&nbsp;for the same period in 2023. The year-over-year decrease was primarily related to decreases in directors&#8217; and officers&#8217; insurance premiums, decreases in finance and accounting fees, primarily due to a decrease in fees from consultants, advisors, and other financial vendors, and decreases in stock-based compensation expense.</p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">Clene reported a net loss of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="26x1" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="20" id="led391591F20246301722379792077" originalfact="$6,785,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$6.8 million</a>, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="34x1" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="20" id="led391591F20246301722379802725">$1.06</a>&nbsp;per share, for the quarter ended&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="20" id="led391585F2023771691438223925" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">June 30, 2024</a>, compared to a net loss of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="26x2" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="20" id="led391591F20246301722379813967" originalfact="$25,143,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$25.1 million</a>, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="34x2" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="20" id="led391591F20246301722379821928">$5.84</a>&nbsp;per share, for the same period in&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="20" id="led391585F2023771691438229471" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">2023</a>.</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;"><b>About Clene</b></div>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">Clene Inc., (Nasdaq: CLNN) (along with its subsidiaries, &#8220;Clene&#8221;) and its wholly owned subsidiary Clene Nanomedicine Inc., is a late clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on improving mitochondrial health and protecting neuronal function to treat neurodegenerative diseases, including amyotrophic lateral sclerosis, Parkinson&#8217;s disease and multiple sclerosis. CNM-Au8<sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">&#174;</sup> is an investigational first-in-class therapy that improves central nervous system cells&#8217; survival and function via a mechanism that targets mitochondrial function and the NAD pathway while reducing oxidative stress. CNM-Au8<sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">&#174;</sup> is a federally registered trademark of Clene Nanomedicine, Inc. The company is based in Salt Lake City, Utah, with R&amp;D and manufacturing operations in Maryland. For more information, please visit www.clene.com or follow us on X and LinkedIn.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><b>About CNM-Au8<sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">&#174;</sup></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">CNM-Au8 is an oral suspension of gold nanocrystals developed to restore neuronal health and function by increasing energy production and utilization. The catalytically active nanocrystals of CNM-Au8 drive critical cellular energy producing reactions that enable neuroprotection and remyelination by increasing neuronal and glial resilience to disease-relevant stressors. CNM-Au8<sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">&#174;</sup> is a federally registered trademark of Clene Nanomedicine Inc.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;</p>
